330.18(1): tsho'i ngos nas kyang da res las don chen po 'grub pa'i gdeng spobs dang dad gus lhag 
330.19(1): bsam bcas sngar las lhag par 'phel song / rig pa'i gnas dang bstan pa'i bon 
330.20(1): gyis phyug pa'i phyi mo g.yung drung bon gyi gzhung lugs la grub mtha' 'dzin pa mi chen bla 
330.21(1): chen 'gas gcig rjes gnyis 'jug gis bsam bzhin du brda chad khag log 'grel 
330.22(1): byas te rjes 'dzin rnams mgo rmongs su bcug pa mthong / 'di dag ni rgyal khab dang mi 
331.1(1): rigs/ chos lugs bcas gang la yang mthun sgril dang bde skyid kyi bkag rdo ru 'gyur 
331.2(1): gshis/ 'dir bon gyi gzhung lugs ngo ma shes 'dod na bon gyi gsung rab dpe cha 'di 
331.3(1): lta bu la blta klog dang zhib 'jug gnang re'i ched dang / g.yung drung bon gyi bla sprul 
331.4(1): mkhas dbang mang pos yun ring re bskul byas pa'i rkyen dang / rgya che'i bod yig klog 
331.5(1): pa po yongs la blta bde 'khyer sla'i cha rkyen du dmigs nas/ ston pa'i gsung rab lung 
331.6(1): gi bon rin po che'i skor deb phreng brgya dang lnga bcu can zhig yig dkar gyi lam nas 
331.7(1): legs bsgrigs byas te/ rje smra seng bla ma'i gsung gi byin rlabs las 'phos pa/ g.yung

331.12(1): gang du bsdur ba/ bsdur ba'i legs cha gang zhig thon pa sogs glegs bam so so'i nang 
331.13(1): dang mjug gi zhus bsgrigs gsal bshad du bris yod/ mdor na nged las mi yongs 
331.14(1): kyis spyi lo 2011lo nas bzung mi lo lnga yi ring dad pa dag snang dang rang gi dge sbyor 
331.15(1): dang bstan la zhabs phyi gtso bzung thog deb rer tshar grangs bco lnga nas nyi shu bar 
331.16(1): zhus dag byas yod pas sngar las lhag pa'i legs cha zhig thon yod pa'i re ba yod/ 'on 
331.17(1): kyang re 'ga' ma dpe gcig ma gtogs bsdur ya ma rnyed pa dang / re 'ga' bsdur ya 
331.18(1): du ma rnyed kyang bris pa'i chad lhag sogs kyis gcig mtshungs med pa dang / nged zhus 
331.19(1): sgrig pa tsho'i mkhyen dpyod tshad brgal can min pa bcas dang rjes 'gro byas pas nor 
331.20(1): 'khrul gyis bslad pa'ang yod nges pas/ rjes gzigs mkhan rnam pas su dang gang la 
331.21(1): khag dkri med pa rang bstan rang skyong gi 'gan 'khri gtsang ma phrag tu khur ste bstan pa 
331.22(1): rin po che'i ched du nor 'khrul yo bsrang dag ther gnang ba'i skul ma zhu rgyu dang /
332.1(1): mthar don du nged [<<]g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang [>>]
332.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
332.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
332.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
332.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
332.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
332.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
332.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
332.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan [(3) ]bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
332.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
332.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
332.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
332.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
332.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
332.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
332.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
332.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i
